aboue speciall prerogatiue therin anthony vndoubtedly true yet good cosyn moste base kynde hath moe cause comfort haue spoke yet haue wote well kynde sent v synne spoken none comforte yet twayn witte one refrayneth v synne el woulde fall serueth v merite christes passio meane whiche god kepeth v hell serueth satisfaccion suche payne el shoulde endure purgatorye howbeit therin great cause ioye besides surely paine sent v sinnes whatsoeuer wise happen vnto v synne neuer sore neuer open euidente vnto oure selfe worlde yet praye grace take mekely paciently confessing god farre ouer litle fault beseche hym yet neuerthelesse yt sith shall come hence void al good workes wherof haue reward heaue bee onely mercyfull v take oure presente tribulacion reliefe oure paynes purgatory also gracious high price vpon poore thing price god setteth throughe christes passion also orkes v good workes godwarde woorketh man without god woorke graunte also man maye proude woorkes owne vnperfecte woorkyng al manne maye doe doe god good seruaunte vnprofitable dooeth bare duetye say graunt vnto thinges one thyng twayne doe graunt v agayne menne bounde woorke good workes haue tyme power whoso woorketh true fayth moste shall moste rewarded set thei therto al rewardes shal geuen hym fayth alone nothing hys woorkes beecause hys fayth thyng saye forceth worke well stryue wyll matter yet trust greate sauyoure sayeth vobis qui ridetis nunc quia lugebitis flebitis woe maye bee laughe nowe shall wayle wepe est tempus flendi sayeth scrypture est tempus ridendi tyme wepyng tyme laughyng see setteth weping tyme tyme wretched worlde laughynge shall come heauen also tyme sowyng time reapyng nowe must thys worlde sowe wee maye worlde reape shorte sowyng tyme thys wepyng worlde muste water oure sede showres oure teares shall haue heauen merye laughyng harueste euer euntes ibant flebant saith prophete mittentes semina sua wente foorth sowed theyr seedes wepyng sayeth shall folow therof venie te autem venient cum exultacione po ta te manipulos suo shall come agayne laughing wyth greate ioye exultacion theyr handes full corne theyr handes loe theyr goyng home towardes heauen sowe theyr sede wepyng shall daye iudgemente come theyr body agayne wyth euerlastyng plentye laughyng proue thys lyfe laughyng tyme rather time wepyng finde oure sauiour hymselfe weped twyse thryse neuer fynde laughed much wyll sweare neuer ye least wise lefte v ensa ple syde lefte v ensaumple weping wepyng haue matter inough bothe oure owne synnes folkes surelye shoulde dooe bewayle theyr wretched synnes houre descende theyr graue paynefullye buryed hell saincte paule sayeth vnto hebrues god loueth chastyseth et flagellat omnem filium quem recipit scourgeth euerye sonne hys receyueth sayncte paule sayeth also per multas tr bulaciones oportet no introire regnum dei manye trybulacyons muste goe kingdome god meruayle oure sauiour christ sayd selfe vnto hys two dysciples wer goyng castle emaus nesciebatis quia oportebat christum pati sic introire regnum su knowe christe muste suffer goe hys kyngdome woulde wee seruauntes looke priuiledge oure maysters house oure maister selfe would eat hys kyngdome ease hymselfe gote owne payne hys kyngdom hath ordayned hys discyples sayeth vnto v qui v lt esse meus discipulus tollat crucem suam sequatur anye manne wyll disciple lette hym learne dooe haue done take crosse trybulacion vpon backe folowe saieth loe lette hym laughe make merye nowe heauen serue chrystes dysciples thei take theyr crosse trybulacyon shall folke come neuer haue tribulacyon true saincte paule saieth god chastyseth loueth scourgeth euerye chylde whome receyueth heauen shall none come suche loueth receyueth whan shall come thyther neuer chastyseth neuer dooeth vouchesafe fyle hys handes vpon geue muche one lashe yf wee saincte paule sayeth come heauen manye trybulacions howe shal come thither neuer haue none thus see well verye scripture selfe howe true woordes olde holye sainctes wyth one voyce maner saye al one thing wit shall haue bothe contynuall wealth thys worlde therefore syth thys worlde without anye trybulacion enioye long continuall course neuer interrupted prosperitie haue great cause feare discoumforte lest bee farre fallen god fauor stande depe indignacion displeasure whyle neuer sendeth trybulacion whiche euer wonte sende whome loueth therefore saye trybulacion haue syde greate cause take theyr gryefe great inwarde coumforte spyrytuall consolacion pthe xiiii chapter certaine obieccion ansvver therto vincent verelye good vncle thys semeth dede howbeit yet thynke saye verye sore thynges concernyng suche person contynuall prosperitie wote well fewe also haue rule aucthoritye thys worlde theyr hande wote well talke suche greate connyng menne trowe tell trueth aske whyther whyle make merye earth theyr lyfe maye yet haue heauen doe tel yes yes well ynough haue heard tell selfe antony suppose good cosyn wyse man specially none good therewith tell man fully fashyon surely say feare flatter either lucre feare thinke peraduenture thus man maketh muche geueth money also faste watche praye feare would doe goe tell nowe doe hym serue goe faste watche praie himselfe sette therto saye farther diligente intercession hym trust ye meane god soner geue grace amende fast watche praye take affliccion owne body bettering hys synfull soule woulde bee wonderous wroth would loth haue grace make leaue mirth sitte mourne synne suche minde lo haue vnlerned haue worldly wit wil tell great men suche tale perilously beguile fainte hearte afrayed nedeth reaso whereof f yeth often tymes feare thing fledde shoulde take harme man dooeth tyme fleing make enemy bolde would fled durst abyde therby geue ouer ee fault pusillanimitie maketh manne tribulacion fieble heart firste impacient afterwarde often tymes driueth impacience contrarye affeccion making frowardlye stubburne angry againste god thereby fall blasphemye dooe damned soules hell faulte pusillanimitie timerouse mynd letteth man also many time ye many good thinges whiche tooke good omake trust goddes helpe well able dooe deuill casteth cowardise maketh take humilitie thinke selfe vnmete vnable thereto therefore leaue good thing vndone whereof god offereth hym occasyon made hym mete conueniente thereto suche folke haue nede lyfte vp scrupulous conscience thys pusillanimytie bryngeth forthe nyghtes feare verye tymerous daughter sely wretched gyrle euer puling called scrupulosytie scrupulous conscience thys gyrle metely good pussell house neuer idle euer occupied busy albeit haue verye gentle maystres yt loueth wel well content wyth doeth well alwayes wel content pardon doeth felowes letteth knowe wyll yet peuishe gyrle neuer cease whining puling feare leste maystres alwaye angry wyth yt shal shrewdly shent maistres wene lyke cotent condicion naye verely knewe one selfe whose maystres verye wyse woman whiche thing woman rare verye mylde also meeke liked verye well suche seruice dyd house continuall dyscomfortable fashio much misliked woulde sometyme saye eygh ayleth gyrle eluishe vrchyn weneth deuill trow suerly x time better seruice doeth yet wyth fantastical feare woulde loth haue house thus fareth loe scrupulous perso frameth selfe many tymes double feare hathe cause many tymes great feare cause al whiche dede sinne maketh veniall venial imagineth deadlye yet falleth beyng namely theyr nature long liueth without tha feareth neuer ful confessed neuer full cotryte sinnes neuer full forgeuen
